           return WitnessResult(support=0.01, log_likelihood=-50, ...)

```python # Coverage Witness (1 week effort) class CoverageWitness(Witness): """Uniform coverage expected; spikes = collapsed repeats.""" def init(self, coverage_array, block_positions, resolution): self.expected = np.median(coverage_array[coverage_array > 0])

   def evaluate_adjacency(self, ...):
       # Coverage discontinuity at junction = evidence against
       ratio = max(cov_a, cov_b) / max(min(cov_a, cov_b), 1)
       if ratio > 2.0:
           support = 0.3  # Evidence against

```

     1‚Üí"""
     2‚ÜíBase classes for witnesses.
     3‚Üí
     4‚ÜíA Witness converts raw evidence into likelihood functions.
     5‚ÜíEach witness type implements the same interface but computes
     6‚Üílikelihoods from different evidence sources.
     7‚Üí"""
     8‚Üí
     9‚Üífrom __future__ import annotations
    10‚Üí
    11‚Üífrom abc import ABC, abstractmethod
    12‚Üífrom dataclasses import dataclass, field
    13‚Üífrom typing import Any, Optional, Protocol
    14‚Üí
    15‚Üíimport numpy as np
    16‚Üífrom numpy.typing import NDArray
    17‚Üí
    18‚Üí
    19‚Üí@dataclass
    20‚Üíclass WitnessResult:
    21‚Üí    """
    22‚Üí    Result from a witness computation.
    23‚Üí
    24‚Üí    Contains the support score (0-1) and detailed metrics
    25‚Üí    for a specific structural decision.
    26‚Üí    """
    27‚Üí
    28‚Üí    # Overall support score (0-1, higher = more support)
    29‚Üí    support: float
    30‚Üí
    31‚Üí    # Log-likelihood of the observed evidence given the arrangement
    32‚Üí    log_likelihood: float
    33‚Üí
    34‚Üí    # Detailed metrics (witness-specific)
    35‚Üí    metrics: dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)
    36‚Üí
    37‚Üí    # Human-readable explanation
    38‚Üí    explanation: Optional[str] = None
    39‚Üí
    40‚Üí    def validate(self) -> list[str]:
    41‚Üí        """Validate the result."""
    42‚Üí        errors = []
    43‚Üí        if not 0.0 <= self.support <= 1.0:
    44‚Üí            errors.append(f"support must be in [0, 1], got {self.support}")
    45‚Üí        if np.isnan(self.log_likelihood):
    46‚Üí            errors.append("log_likelihood is NaN")
    47‚Üí        return errors
    48‚Üí
    49‚Üí
    50‚Üíclass Witness(ABC):
    51‚Üí    """
    52‚Üí    Abstract base class for witnesses.
    53‚Üí
    54‚Üí    A witness computes P(evidence | arrangement) for a specific
    55‚Üí    type of evidence. Witnesses don't make decisions; they
    56‚Üí    provide likelihood scores that the inference engine combines.
    57‚Üí    """
    58‚Üí
    59‚Üí    @property
    60‚Üí    @abstractmethod
    61‚Üí    def name(self) -> str:
    62‚Üí        """Name of this witness type."""
    63‚Üí        ...

    72‚Üí        orientation: str,
    73‚Üí    ) -> WitnessResult:
    74‚Üí        """
    75‚Üí        Evaluate evidence for a proposed adjacency.
    76‚Üí
    77‚Üí        Args:
    78‚Üí            block_a: First block ID

    80‚Üí            block_b: Second block ID
    81‚Üí            end_b: End of second block ("5prime" or "3prime")
    82‚Üí            orientation: Orientation string ("++", "+-", "-+", "--")
    83‚Üí

    85‚Üí            WitnessResult with support score and log-likelihood

/Users/scotthandley/Code/pretextview-update/verity/witness/telomere.py
"""
Telomere Witness Module

Evaluates telomere positioning constraints for genome assembly validation.

Telomeres are repetitive sequences at chromosome ends. Their presence
mid-chromosome indicates a misjoin. Their absence at chromosome ends
suggests incomplete assembly.

Biology:
- Vertebrates: (TTAGGG)n
- Plants: (TTTAGGG)n
- Most eukaryotes: G-rich 3' overhang
- Fungi/some others: variable motifs

This witness requires NO training data - purely biological constraints.
"""

from __future__ import annotations

import re
from dataclasses import dataclass, field
from enum import Enum
from typing import Any, Optional, Iterator

import numpy as np
from numpy.typing import NDArray

from verity.witness.base import Witness, WitnessResult


# Common telomere motifs by taxonomic group
TELOMERE_MOTIFS = {
    "vertebrate": "TTAGGG",
    "plant": "TTTAGGG",
    "insect": "TTAGG",
    "nematode": "TTAGGC",
    "ciliate_tetrahymena": "TTGGGG",
    "ciliate_paramecium": "TTGGG",
    "yeast_saccharomyces": "TG{1,3}",  # Irregular
    "default": "TTAGGG",  # Most common
}


class TelomereStrand(str, Enum):
    """Strand orientation of telomere repeat."""
    FORWARD = "forward"   # G-rich strand (TTAGGG)
    REVERSE = "reverse"   # C-rich strand (CCCTAA)


@dataclass
class TelomereHit:
    """A detected telomere repeat region."""

    contig: str
    start: int  # 0-based start position
    end: int    # 0-based end position (exclusive)
    strand: TelomereStrand
    repeat_count: int  # Number of tandem repeats
    motif: str  # The motif that matched

    @property
    def length(self) -> int:
        """Length of the telomere region in bp."""
        return self.end - self.start

    @property
    def position_type(self) -> str:
        """Classify position as 'start', 'end', or 'internal'."""
        # This will be set by the caller based on contig length
        return "unknown"

    def to_dict(self) -> dict[str, Any]:
        """Convert to dictionary."""
        return {
            "contig": self.contig,
            "start": self.start,
            "end": self.end,
            "strand": self.strand.value,
            "repeat_count": self.repeat_count,
            "motif": self.motif,
            "length": self.length,
        }


@dataclass
class BlockPosition:
    """Position of a block within the assembly coordinate system."""

    contig: str
    start: int  # Start position in contig (bp)
    end: int    # End position in contig (bp)

    @property
    def length(self) -> int:
        """Length of block in bp."""
        return self.end - self.start


def reverse_complement(seq: str) -> str:
    """Compute reverse complement of a DNA sequence."""
    complement = {"A": "T", "T": "A", "G": "C", "C": "G",
                  "a": "t", "t": "a", "g": "c", "c": "g",
                  "N": "N", "n": "n"}
    return "".join(complement.get(base, "N") for base in reversed(seq))


class TelomereWitness(Witness):
    """
    Witness for telomere positioning constraints.

    Evaluates whether telomere positions are consistent with
    a valid chromosome structure:

    1. Telomeres should appear at chromosome ends
    2. Telomeres should NOT appear mid-chromosome (indicates misjoin)
    3. A complete chromosome should have exactly 2 telomeres

    This witness uses ONLY biological constraints - no training data.
    """

    def __init__(
        self,
        sequences: dict[str, str],  # contig_id -> sequence
        block_positions: dict[str, BlockPosition],
        motif: str = "TTAGGG",
        min_repeats: int = 3,
        search_window: int = 10000,  # bp from ends to search
        internal_penalty: float = -50.0,  # log-likelihood penalty for internal telomere
    ):
        """
        Initialize the telomere witness.

        Args:
            sequences: Dictionary mapping contig IDs to sequences
            block_positions: Dictionary mapping block IDs to positions
            motif: Telomere repeat motif (default: vertebrate)
            min_repeats: Minimum tandem repeats to count as telomere
            search_window: How far from contig ends to search (bp)
            internal_penalty: Log-likelihood penalty for internal telomeres
        """
        self.sequences = sequences
        self.block_positions = block_positions
        self.motif = motif
        self.reverse_motif = reverse_complement(motif)
        self.min_repeats = min_repeats
        self.search_window = search_window
        self.internal_penalty = internal_penalty

        # Compute contig lengths
        self.contig_lengths = {
            contig: len(seq) for contig, seq in sequences.items()
        }

        # Find all telomere locations
        self.telomere_hits = self._find_all_telomeres()

        # Index telomeres by block
        self.block_telomeres = self._index_telomeres_by_block()

    @property
    def name(self) -> str:
        """Name of this witness type."""
        return "telomere"

    def _find_all_telomeres(self) -> list[TelomereHit]:
        """Find all telomere regions across all contigs."""
        hits = []

        for contig_id, sequence in self.sequences.items():
            contig_hits = self._find_telomeres_in_sequence(contig_id, sequence)
            hits.extend(contig_hits)

        return hits

    def _find_telomeres_in_sequence(
        self,
        contig_id: str,
        sequence: str,
    ) -> list[TelomereHit]:
        """Find telomere repeats in a single sequence."""
        hits = []
        seq_upper = sequence.upper()

        # Build regex pattern for tandem repeats
        # Match at least min_repeats consecutive copies
        forward_pattern = f"({self.motif}){{{self.min_repeats},}}"
        reverse_pattern = f"({self.reverse_motif}){{{self.min_repeats},}}"

        # Search for forward strand (G-rich)
        for match in re.finditer(forward_pattern, seq_upper, re.IGNORECASE):
            repeat_count = len(match.group(0)) // len(self.motif)
            hits.append(TelomereHit(
                contig=contig_id,
                start=match.start(),
                end=match.end(),
                strand=TelomereStrand.FORWARD,
                repeat_count=repeat_count,
                motif=self.motif,
            ))

        # Search for reverse strand (C-rich)
        for match in re.finditer(reverse_pattern, seq_upper, re.IGNORECASE):
            repeat_count = len(match.group(0)) // len(self.reverse_motif)
            hits.append(TelomereHit(
                contig=contig_id,
                start=match.start(),
                end=match.end(),
                strand=TelomereStrand.REVERSE,
                repeat_count=repeat_count,
                motif=self.reverse_motif,
            ))

        return hits

    def _index_telomeres_by_block(self) -> dict[str, list[TelomereHit]]:
        """Index telomere hits by block ID."""
        block_telomeres: dict[str, list[TelomereHit]] = {
            block_id: [] for block_id in self.block_positions
        }

        for hit in self.telomere_hits:
            # Find which block(s) this telomere falls in
            for block_id, pos in self.block_positions.items():
                if pos.contig != hit.contig:
                    continue

                # Check if telomere overlaps block
                if hit.start < pos.end and hit.end > pos.start:
                    block_telomeres[block_id].append(hit)

        return block_telomeres

    def _is_at_contig_end(
        self,
        hit: TelomereHit,
        which_end: str = "either",
    ) -> bool:
        """
        Check if a telomere hit is at a contig end.

        Args:
            hit: The telomere hit to check
            which_end: "start", "end", or "either"

        Returns:
            True if telomere is within search_window of specified end
        """
        contig_length = self.contig_lengths.get(hit.contig, 0)

        at_start = hit.start < self.search_window
        at_end = hit.end > contig_length - self.search_window

        if which_end == "start":
            return at_start
        elif which_end == "end":
            return at_end
        else:  # "either"
            return at_start or at_end

    def _is_internal_telomere(self, hit: TelomereHit) -> bool:
        """Check if telomere is internal (not at contig end)."""
        return not self._is_at_contig_end(hit)

    def _get_block_end_telomeres(
        self,
        block_id: str,
        end: str,  # "5prime" or "3prime"
    ) -> list[TelomereHit]:
        """Get telomeres near a specific block end."""
        if block_id not in self.block_positions:
            return []

        pos = self.block_positions[block_id]
        block_telomeres = self.block_telomeres.get(block_id, [])

        end_telomeres = []
        for hit in block_telomeres:
            if end == "5prime":
                # Check if near start of block
                distance_to_start = hit.start - pos.start
                if abs(distance_to_start) < self.search_window:
                    end_telomeres.append(hit)
            else:  # 3prime
                # Check if near end of block
                distance_to_end = pos.end - hit.end
                if abs(distance_to_end) < self.search_window:
                    end_telomeres.append(hit)

        return end_telomeres

    def evaluate_adjacency(
        self,
        block_a: str,
        end_a: str,
        block_b: str,
        end_b: str,
        orientation: str,
    ) -> WitnessResult:
        """
        Evaluate telomere evidence for a proposed adjacency.

        Telomeres at a junction = STRONG evidence AGAINST adjacency.
        (You cannot join two chromosome ends!)

        Args:
            block_a: First block ID
            end_a: End of first block ("5prime" or "3prime")
            block_b: Second block ID
            end_b: End of second block ("5prime" or "3prime")
            orientation: Orientation string ("++", "+-", "-+", "--")

        Returns:
            WitnessResult with support score and log-likelihood
        """
        # Get telomeres at the junction ends
        telomeres_a = self._get_block_end_telomeres(block_a, end_a)
        telomeres_b = self._get_block_end_telomeres(block_b, end_b)

        # Count telomeres at junction
        n_telomeres_a = len(telomeres_a)
        n_telomeres_b = len(telomeres_b)
        total_telomeres = n_telomeres_a + n_telomeres_b

        # Build explanation
        explanation_parts = []

        if total_telomeres == 0:
            # No telomeres at junction - uninformative
            support = 0.5
            log_likelihood = 0.0
            explanation = "No telomeres at junction - uninformative"

        elif total_telomeres == 1:
            # One telomere - moderate evidence against
            # (One side is a chromosome end)
            support = 0.2
            log_likelihood = self.internal_penalty / 2
            which_side = "block_a" if n_telomeres_a > 0 else "block_b"
            explanation = f"Telomere at {which_side} end - likely chromosome terminus"

        else:
            # Two telomeres - strong evidence against
            # (Both sides are chromosome ends - impossible adjacency)
            support = 0.01
            log_likelihood = self.internal_penalty
            explanation = "Telomeres at both junction ends - cannot be adjacent"

        return WitnessResult(
            support=support,
            log_likelihood=log_likelihood,
            metrics={
                "telomeres_at_block_a": n_telomeres_a,
                "telomeres_at_block_b": n_telomeres_b,
                "total_telomeres_at_junction": total_telomeres,
            },
            explanation=explanation,
        )

    def evaluate_chromosome_assignment(
        self,
        block_id: str,
        chromosome_blocks: list[str],
    ) -> WitnessResult:
        """
        Evaluate telomere evidence for chromosome assignment.

        A complete chromosome should have exactly 2 telomeres (both ends).

        Args:
            block_id: Block to evaluate
            chromosome_blocks: Other blocks assigned to this chromosome

        Returns:
            WitnessResult with support score and log-likelihood
        """
        # Count telomeres in this block
        block_telomeres = self.block_telomeres.get(block_id, [])
        n_telomeres = len(block_telomeres)

        # Count total telomeres in chromosome
        all_blocks = [block_id] + chromosome_blocks
        total_telomeres = sum(
            len(self.block_telomeres.get(bid, []))
            for bid in all_blocks
        )

        # Count terminal vs internal telomeres
        terminal_count = 0
        internal_count = 0
        for bid in all_blocks:
            for hit in self.block_telomeres.get(bid, []):
                if self._is_at_contig_end(hit):
                    terminal_count += 1
                else:
                    internal_count += 1

        # Evaluate based on telomere count
        if internal_count > 0:
            # Internal telomeres are problematic
            support = 0.2
            log_likelihood = self.internal_penalty * internal_count
            explanation = f"Found {internal_count} internal telomere(s) - possible misjoin"
        elif total_telomeres == 2 and terminal_count == 2:
            # Perfect: exactly 2 terminal telomeres
            support = 0.9
            log_likelihood = 10.0  # Positive evidence
            explanation = "Chromosome has 2 terminal telomeres - complete"
        elif total_telomeres == 1:
            # One telomere - incomplete chromosome
            support = 0.6
            log_likelihood = 0.0
            explanation = "Chromosome has 1 telomere - may be incomplete"
        elif total_telomeres == 0:
            # No telomeres - uninformative or incomplete
            support = 0.5
            log_likelihood = 0.0
            explanation = "No telomeres found - may be incomplete or acrocentric"
        else:
            # More than 2 telomeres - problematic
            support = 0.3
            log_likelihood = self.internal_penalty / 2
            explanation = f"Found {total_telomeres} telomeres - possible assembly error"

        return WitnessResult(
            support=support,
            log_likelihood=log_likelihood,
            metrics={
                "block_telomeres": n_telomeres,
                "chromosome_total_telomeres": total_telomeres,
                "terminal_telomeres": terminal_count,
                "internal_telomeres": internal_count,
            },
            explanation=explanation,
        )

    def detect_internal_telomeres(self) -> list[tuple[str, TelomereHit]]:
        """
        Find all internal telomeres (likely misjoins).

        Returns:
            List of (block_id, TelomereHit) for internal telomeres
        """
        internal = []
        for block_id, hits in self.block_telomeres.items():
            for hit in hits:
                if self._is_internal_telomere(hit):
                    internal.append((block_id, hit))
        return internal

    def get_telomere_summary(self) -> dict[str, Any]:
        """Get summary statistics about telomere detection."""
        total_hits = len(self.telomere_hits)

        terminal_hits = sum(
            1 for hit in self.telomere_hits
            if self._is_at_contig_end(hit)
        )
        internal_hits = total_hits - terminal_hits

        # Count by strand
        forward_count = sum(
            1 for hit in self.telomere_hits
            if hit.strand == TelomereStrand.FORWARD
        )
        reverse_count = total_hits - forward_count

        return {
            "total_telomeres": total_hits,
            "terminal_telomeres": terminal_hits,
            "internal_telomeres": internal_hits,
            "forward_strand": forward_count,
            "reverse_strand": reverse_count,
            "motif": self.motif,
            "min_repeats": self.min_repeats,
            "search_window": self.search_window,
            "contigs_searched": len(self.sequences),
            "blocks_indexed": len(self.block_positions),
        }

    def get_parameters(self) -> dict[str, Any]:
        """Get the parameters used by this witness."""
        return {
            "witness_type": "telomere",
            "motif": self.motif,
            "reverse_motif": self.reverse_motif,
            "min_repeats": self.min_repeats,
            "search_window": self.search_window,
            "internal_penalty": self.internal_penalty,
            "contigs": list(self.sequences.keys()),
            "blocks": list(self.block_positions.keys()),
        }


def create_telomere_witness_from_fasta(
    fasta_path: str,
    block_positions: dict[str, BlockPosition],
    motif: str = "TTAGGG",
    min_repeats: int = 3,
    search_window: int = 10000,
) -> TelomereWitness:
    """
    Create a TelomereWitness from a FASTA file.

    Args:
        fasta_path: Path to FASTA file
        block_positions: Dictionary mapping block IDs to positions
        motif: Telomere repeat motif
        min_repeats: Minimum tandem repeats
        search_window: Search window from contig ends

    Returns:
        Configured TelomereWitness instance
    """
    # Try to use pyfaidx for indexed access
    try:
        import pyfaidx
        fasta = pyfaidx.Fasta(fasta_path)
        sequences = {name: str(fasta[name]) for name in fasta.keys()}
    except ImportError:
        # Fall back to simple parsing
        sequences = _parse_fasta_simple(fasta_path)

    return TelomereWitness(
        sequences=sequences,
        block_positions=block_positions,
        motif=motif,
        min_repeats=min_repeats,
        search_window=search_window,
    )


def _parse_fasta_simple(fasta_path: str) -> dict[str, str]:
    """Simple FASTA parser without dependencies."""
    sequences = {}
    current_name = None
    current_seq = []

    with open(fasta_path, 'r') as f:
        for line in f:
            line = line.strip()
            if line.startswith('>'):
                if current_name is not None:
                    sequences[current_name] = ''.join(current_seq)
                current_name = line[1:].split()[0]  # First word after >
                current_seq = []
            else:
                current_seq.append(line)

        # Don't forget the last sequence
        if current_name is not None:
            sequences[current_name] = ''.join(current_seq)

    return sequences

"""Tests for verity.witness.telomere module."""

import pytest
import numpy as np

from verity.witness.base import WitnessResult
from verity.witness.telomere import (
    TelomereWitness,
    TelomereHit,
    TelomereStrand,
    BlockPosition,
    TELOMERE_MOTIFS,
    reverse_complement,
    _parse_fasta_simple,
)


class TestReverseComplement:
    """Tests for reverse_complement function."""

    def test_simple_sequence(self):
        """Test basic reverse complement."""
        assert reverse_complement("ATCG") == "CGAT"

    def test_telomere_motif(self):
        """Test vertebrate telomere motif."""
        assert reverse_complement("TTAGGG") == "CCCTAA"

    def test_lowercase(self):
        """Test lowercase handling."""
        assert reverse_complement("atcg") == "cgat"

    def test_empty(self):
        """Test empty sequence."""
        assert reverse_complement("") == ""

    def test_with_n(self):
        """Test sequence with N."""
        assert reverse_complement("ATNGC") == "GCNAT"


class TestTelomereHit:
    """Tests for TelomereHit dataclass."""

    def test_basic_creation(self):
        """Test basic hit creation."""
        hit = TelomereHit(
            contig="chr1",
            start=0,
            end=18,
            strand=TelomereStrand.FORWARD,
            repeat_count=3,
            motif="TTAGGG",
        )
        assert hit.contig == "chr1"
        assert hit.start == 0
        assert hit.end == 18
        assert hit.strand == TelomereStrand.FORWARD
        assert hit.repeat_count == 3
        assert hit.motif == "TTAGGG"

    def test_length_property(self):
        """Test length calculation."""
        hit = TelomereHit(
            contig="chr1",
            start=100,
            end=150,
            strand=TelomereStrand.FORWARD,
            repeat_count=8,
            motif="TTAGGG",
        )
        assert hit.length == 50

    def test_to_dict(self):
        """Test serialization to dict."""
        hit = TelomereHit(
            contig="chr1",
            start=0,
            end=30,
            strand=TelomereStrand.REVERSE,
            repeat_count=5,
            motif="CCCTAA",
        )
        d = hit.to_dict()
        assert d["contig"] == "chr1"
        assert d["start"] == 0
        assert d["end"] == 30
        assert d["strand"] == "reverse"
        assert d["repeat_count"] == 5
        assert d["length"] == 30


class TestTelomereWitness:
    """Tests for TelomereWitness class."""

    @pytest.fixture
    def simple_sequences(self):
        """Create simple test sequences with telomeres."""
        # Create a 50kb sequence with telomeres at both ends
        telomere_fwd = "TTAGGG" * 10  # 60bp forward telomere
        telomere_rev = "CCCTAA" * 10  # 60bp reverse telomere
        middle = "ATCG" * 12435  # ~50kb middle sequence

        return {
            "contig1": telomere_fwd + middle + telomere_rev,
        }

    @pytest.fixture
    def simple_blocks(self):
        """Create simple block positions."""
        return {
            "block_A": BlockPosition(contig="contig1", start=0, end=25000),
            "block_B": BlockPosition(contig="contig1", start=25000, end=50000),
        }

    @pytest.fixture
    def witness(self, simple_sequences, simple_blocks):
        """Create a TelomereWitness for testing."""
        return TelomereWitness(
            sequences=simple_sequences,
            block_positions=simple_blocks,
            motif="TTAGGG",
            min_repeats=3,
            search_window=10000,
        )

    def test_initialization(self, witness):
        """Test witness initialization."""
        assert witness.name == "telomere"
        assert witness.motif == "TTAGGG"
        assert witness.reverse_motif == "CCCTAA"
        assert witness.min_repeats == 3
        assert witness.search_window == 10000

    def test_find_telomeres_forward(self):
        """Test finding forward telomere repeats."""
        sequences = {
            "test": "ATCG" + "TTAGGG" * 5 + "GCTA",  # 5 repeats in middle
        }
        blocks = {
            "block1": BlockPosition(contig="test", start=0, end=len(sequences["test"])),
        }
        witness = TelomereWitness(
            sequences=sequences,
            block_positions=blocks,
            min_repeats=3,
        )

        assert len(witness.telomere_hits) == 1
        hit = witness.telomere_hits[0]
        assert hit.strand == TelomereStrand.FORWARD
        assert hit.repeat_count == 5
        assert hit.start == 4
        assert hit.end == 34

    def test_find_telomeres_reverse(self):
        """Test finding reverse telomere repeats."""
        sequences = {
            "test": "ATCG" + "CCCTAA" * 4 + "GCTA",  # 4 repeats
        }
        blocks = {
            "block1": BlockPosition(contig="test", start=0, end=len(sequences["test"])),
        }
        witness = TelomereWitness(
            sequences=sequences,
            block_positions=blocks,
            min_repeats=3,
        )

        assert len(witness.telomere_hits) == 1
        hit = witness.telomere_hits[0]
        assert hit.strand == TelomereStrand.REVERSE
        assert hit.repeat_count == 4

    def test_find_telomeres_both_strands(self):
        """Test finding telomeres on both strands."""
        sequences = {
            "test": "TTAGGG" * 5 + "N" * 100 + "CCCTAA" * 5,
        }
        blocks = {
            "block1": BlockPosition(contig="test", start=0, end=len(sequences["test"])),
        }
        witness = TelomereWitness(
            sequences=sequences,
            block_positions=blocks,
            min_repeats=3,
        )

        assert len(witness.telomere_hits) == 2
        strands = {hit.strand for hit in witness.telomere_hits}
        assert TelomereStrand.FORWARD in strands
        assert TelomereStrand.REVERSE in strands

    def test_min_repeats_threshold(self):
        """Test minimum repeat threshold."""
        sequences = {
            "test": "TTAGGG" * 2 + "NNNN" + "TTAGGG" * 5,  # 2 and 5 repeats
        }
        blocks = {
            "block1": BlockPosition(contig="test", start=0, end=len(sequences["test"])),
        }

        # With min_repeats=3, should only find the 5-repeat stretch
        witness = TelomereWitness(
            sequences=sequences,
            block_positions=blocks,
            min_repeats=3,
        )
        assert len(witness.telomere_hits) == 1
        assert witness.telomere_hits[0].repeat_count == 5

        # With min_repeats=2, should find both
        witness2 = TelomereWitness(
            sequences=sequences,
            block_positions=blocks,
            min_repeats=2,
        )
        assert len(witness2.telomere_hits) == 2

    def test_is_at_contig_end_start(self):
        """Test detection of telomere at contig start."""
        sequences = {
            "test": "TTAGGG" * 10 + "N" * 50000,  # Telomere at start
        }
        blocks = {
            "block1": BlockPosition(contig="test", start=0, end=50060),
        }
        witness = TelomereWitness(
            sequences=sequences,
            block_positions=blocks,
            search_window=10000,
        )

        assert len(witness.telomere_hits) == 1
        hit = witness.telomere_hits[0]
        assert witness._is_at_contig_end(hit, "start") is True
        assert witness._is_at_contig_end(hit, "end") is False
        assert witness._is_at_contig_end(hit, "either") is True

    def test_is_at_contig_end_end(self):
        """Test detection of telomere at contig end."""
        sequences = {
            "test": "N" * 50000 + "CCCTAA" * 10,  # Telomere at end
        }
        blocks = {
            "block1": BlockPosition(contig="test", start=0, end=50060),
        }
        witness = TelomereWitness(
            sequences=sequences,
            block_positions=blocks,
            search_window=10000,
        )

        assert len(witness.telomere_hits) == 1
        hit = witness.telomere_hits[0]
        assert witness._is_at_contig_end(hit, "start") is False
        assert witness._is_at_contig_end(hit, "end") is True
        assert witness._is_at_contig_end(hit, "either") is True

    def test_is_internal_telomere(self):
        """Test detection of internal telomeres."""
        # Telomere in middle of 100kb sequence
        sequences = {
            "test": "N" * 40000 + "TTAGGG" * 10 + "N" * 40000,
        }
        blocks = {
            "block1": BlockPosition(contig="test", start=0, end=80060),
        }
        witness = TelomereWitness(
            sequences=sequences,
            block_positions=blocks,
            search_window=10000,
        )

        assert len(witness.telomere_hits) == 1
        hit = witness.telomere_hits[0]
        assert witness._is_internal_telomere(hit) is True
        assert witness._is_at_contig_end(hit) is False

    def test_evaluate_adjacency_no_telomeres(self):
        """Test adjacency evaluation with no telomeres at junction."""
        sequences = {
            "contig1": "N" * 50000,  # No telomeres
        }
        blocks = {
            "block_A": BlockPosition(contig="contig1", start=0, end=25000),
            "block_B": BlockPosition(contig="contig1", start=25000, end=50000),
        }
        witness = TelomereWitness(
            sequences=sequences,
            block_positions=blocks,
        )

        result = witness.evaluate_adjacency(
            block_a="block_A",
            end_a="3prime",
            block_b="block_B",
            end_b="5prime",
            orientation="++",
        )

        assert isinstance(result, WitnessResult)
        assert result.support == 0.5  # Uninformative
        assert result.log_likelihood == 0.0
        assert "uninformative" in result.explanation.lower()

    def test_evaluate_adjacency_one_telomere(self):
        """Test adjacency evaluation with telomere at one end."""
        # Telomere at junction between blocks
        sequences = {
            "contig1": "N" * 24940 + "TTAGGG" * 10 + "N" * 25000,
        }
        blocks = {
            "block_A": BlockPosition(contig="contig1", start=0, end=25000),
            "block_B": BlockPosition(contig="contig1", start=25000, end=50000),
        }
        witness = TelomereWitness(
            sequences=sequences,
            block_positions=blocks,
            search_window=10000,
        )

        result = witness.evaluate_adjacency(
            block_a="block_A",
            end_a="3prime",
            block_b="block_B",
            end_b="5prime",
            orientation="++",
        )

        assert result.support < 0.5  # Evidence against adjacency
        assert result.support == 0.2
        assert result.metrics["total_telomeres_at_junction"] == 1

    def test_evaluate_adjacency_two_telomeres(self):
        """Test adjacency evaluation with telomeres at both ends."""
        # Telomeres at both junction ends - impossible adjacency
        sequences = {
            "contig1": "N" * 24900 + "TTAGGG" * 10 + "CCCTAA" * 10 + "N" * 24880,
        }
        blocks = {
            "block_A": BlockPosition(contig="contig1", start=0, end=24960),
            "block_B": BlockPosition(contig="contig1", start=24960, end=50000),
        }
        witness = TelomereWitness(
            sequences=sequences,
            block_positions=blocks,
            search_window=10000,
        )

        result = witness.evaluate_adjacency(
            block_a="block_A",
            end_a="3prime",
            block_b="block_B",
            end_b="5prime",
            orientation="++",
        )

        assert result.support == 0.01  # Strong evidence against
        assert result.log_likelihood < -40  # Highly unlikely
        assert "cannot be adjacent" in result.explanation.lower()

    def test_evaluate_chromosome_assignment_complete(self):
        """Test chromosome assignment with complete telomeres."""
        # Perfect chromosome: telomeres at both ends
        sequences = {
            "contig1": "TTAGGG" * 10 + "N" * 49880 + "CCCTAA" * 10,
        }
        blocks = {
            "block_A": BlockPosition(contig="contig1", start=0, end=25000),
            "block_B": BlockPosition(contig="contig1", start=25000, end=50000),
        }
        witness = TelomereWitness(
            sequences=sequences,
            block_positions=blocks,
            search_window=10000,
        )

        result = witness.evaluate_chromosome_assignment(
            block_id="block_A",
            chromosome_blocks=["block_B"],
        )

        assert result.support == 0.9  # High support for complete chromosome
        assert result.log_likelihood > 0  # Positive evidence
        assert result.metrics["terminal_telomeres"] == 2
        assert "complete" in result.explanation.lower()

    def test_evaluate_chromosome_assignment_internal_telomere(self):
        """Test chromosome assignment with internal telomere (misjoin)."""
        # Internal telomere - likely misjoin
        sequences = {
            "contig1": "N" * 24940 + "TTAGGG" * 10 + "N" * 25000,  # Middle telomere
        }
        blocks = {
            "block_A": BlockPosition(contig="contig1", start=0, end=25000),
            "block_B": BlockPosition(contig="contig1", start=25000, end=50000),
        }
        witness = TelomereWitness(
            sequences=sequences,
            block_positions=blocks,
            search_window=10000,
        )

        result = witness.evaluate_chromosome_assignment(
            block_id="block_A",
            chromosome_blocks=["block_B"],
        )

        assert result.support < 0.5  # Evidence against
        assert result.metrics["internal_telomeres"] == 1
        assert "misjoin" in result.explanation.lower()

    def test_detect_internal_telomeres(self):
        """Test detection of all internal telomeres."""
        # Two internal telomeres
        sequences = {
            "contig1": "N" * 20000 + "TTAGGG" * 10 + "N" * 19940 + "CCCTAA" * 10 + "N" * 20000,
        }
        blocks = {
            "block_A": BlockPosition(contig="contig1", start=0, end=40000),
            "block_B": BlockPosition(contig="contig1", start=40000, end=80000),
        }
        witness = TelomereWitness(
            sequences=sequences,
            block_positions=blocks,
            search_window=5000,
        )

        internal = witness.detect_internal_telomeres()
        assert len(internal) == 2

    def test_get_telomere_summary(self, witness):
        """Test telomere summary statistics."""
        summary = witness.get_telomere_summary()

        assert "total_telomeres" in summary
        assert "terminal_telomeres" in summary
        assert "internal_telomeres" in summary
        assert "forward_strand" in summary
        assert "reverse_strand" in summary
        assert summary["motif"] == "TTAGGG"
        assert summary["min_repeats"] == 3

    def test_get_parameters(self, witness):
        """Test parameter retrieval."""
        params = witness.get_parameters()

        assert params["witness_type"] == "telomere"
        assert params["motif"] == "TTAGGG"
        assert params["reverse_motif"] == "CCCTAA"
        assert params["min_repeats"] == 3
        assert params["search_window"] == 10000

    def test_different_motifs(self):
        """Test with different telomere motifs."""
        # Plant telomere motif
        plant_motif = "TTTAGGG"
        sequences = {
            "test": plant_motif * 10 + "N" * 100,
        }
        blocks = {
            "block1": BlockPosition(contig="test", start=0, end=170),
        }
        witness = TelomereWitness(
            sequences=sequences,
            block_positions=blocks,
            motif=plant_motif,
            min_repeats=3,
        )

        assert len(witness.telomere_hits) == 1
        assert witness.telomere_hits[0].motif == plant_motif

    def test_case_insensitivity(self):
        """Test that search is case insensitive."""
        sequences = {
            "test": "ttaggg" * 10 + "N" * 100,  # Lowercase
        }
        blocks = {
            "block1": BlockPosition(contig="test", start=0, end=160),
        }
        witness = TelomereWitness(
            sequences=sequences,
            block_positions=blocks,
            min_repeats=3,
        )

        assert len(witness.telomere_hits) == 1

    def test_empty_sequence(self):
        """Test handling of empty sequence."""
        sequences = {"test": ""}
        blocks = {}
        witness = TelomereWitness(
            sequences=sequences,
            block_positions=blocks,
        )

        assert len(witness.telomere_hits) == 0

    def test_no_telomeres_in_sequence(self):
        """Test sequence with no telomeres."""
        sequences = {
            "test": "ATCGATCGATCG" * 1000,
        }
        blocks = {
            "block1": BlockPosition(contig="test", start=0, end=12000),
        }
        witness = TelomereWitness(
            sequences=sequences,
            block_positions=blocks,
        )

        assert len(witness.telomere_hits) == 0
        summary = witness.get_telomere_summary()
        assert summary["total_telomeres"] == 0


class TestParseFastaSimple:
    """Tests for simple FASTA parser."""

    def test_parse_single_sequence(self, tmp_path):
        """Test parsing single sequence FASTA."""
        fasta_file = tmp_path / "test.fa"
        fasta_file.write_text(">seq1\nATCGATCG\nGCTAGCTA\n")

        sequences = _parse_fasta_simple(str(fasta_file))

        assert "seq1" in sequences
        assert sequences["seq1"] == "ATCGATCGGCTAGCTA"

    def test_parse_multiple_sequences(self, tmp_path):
        """Test parsing multi-sequence FASTA."""
        fasta_file = tmp_path / "test.fa"
        fasta_file.write_text(">seq1\nATCG\n>seq2\nGCTA\n")

        sequences = _parse_fasta_simple(str(fasta_file))

        assert len(sequences) == 2
        assert sequences["seq1"] == "ATCG"
        assert sequences["seq2"] == "GCTA"

    def test_parse_with_description(self, tmp_path):
        """Test parsing FASTA with header descriptions."""
        fasta_file = tmp_path / "test.fa"
        fasta_file.write_text(">seq1 some description here\nATCG\n")

        sequences = _parse_fasta_simple(str(fasta_file))

        assert "seq1" in sequences
        assert sequences["seq1"] == "ATCG"


class TestTelomereMotifs:
    """Tests for predefined telomere motifs."""

    def test_motif_definitions(self):
        """Test that predefined motifs exist."""
        assert "vertebrate" in TELOMERE_MOTIFS
        assert "plant" in TELOMERE_MOTIFS
        assert "insect" in TELOMERE_MOTIFS
        assert "default" in TELOMERE_MOTIFS

    def test_vertebrate_motif(self):
        """Test vertebrate motif is correct."""
        assert TELOMERE_MOTIFS["vertebrate"] == "TTAGGG"

    def test_plant_motif(self):
        """Test plant motif is correct."""
        assert TELOMERE_MOTIFS["plant"] == "TTTAGGG"


class TestEdgeCases:
    """Tests for edge cases and boundary conditions."""

    def test_overlapping_telomeres_with_blocks(self):
        """Test telomere that spans multiple blocks."""
        # Telomere that crosses block boundary
        sequences = {
            "contig1": "N" * 49970 + "TTAGGG" * 10 + "N" * 9970,  # Crosses at 50000
        }
        blocks = {
            "block_A": BlockPosition(contig="contig1", start=0, end=50000),
            "block_B": BlockPosition(contig="contig1", start=50000, end=60000),
        }
        witness = TelomereWitness(
            sequences=sequences,
            block_positions=blocks,
            search_window=10000,
        )

        # Telomere should be indexed for both blocks
        assert len(witness.block_telomeres["block_A"]) >= 1 or len(witness.block_telomeres["block_B"]) >= 1

    def test_very_short_sequence(self):
        """Test handling of very short sequences."""
        sequences = {
            "test": "TTAGGGTTAGGG",  # Only 2 repeats = 12bp
        }
        blocks = {
            "block1": BlockPosition(contig="test", start=0, end=12),
        }
        witness = TelomereWitness(
            sequences=sequences,
            block_positions=blocks,
            min_repeats=3,
        )

        # Should not find telomere (only 2 repeats, need 3)
        assert len(witness.telomere_hits) == 0

    def test_adjacent_telomeres_different_strands(self):
        """Test adjacent telomeres on different strands."""
        sequences = {
            "test": "TTAGGG" * 5 + "CCCTAA" * 5,  # Back-to-back
        }
        blocks = {
            "block1": BlockPosition(contig="test", start=0, end=60),
        }
        witness = TelomereWitness(
            sequences=sequences,
            block_positions=blocks,
            min_repeats=3,
        )

        assert len(witness.telomere_hits) == 2
        strands = {hit.strand for hit in witness.telomere_hits}
        assert len(strands) == 2

    def test_missing_block_in_evaluation(self):
        """Test evaluation with non-existent block."""
        sequences = {"test": "N" * 1000}
        blocks = {
            "block1": BlockPosition(contig="test", start=0, end=500),
        }
        witness = TelomereWitness(
            sequences=sequences,
            block_positions=blocks,
        )

        # Should handle missing block gracefully
        result = witness.evaluate_adjacency(
            block_a="nonexistent",
            end_a="3prime",
            block_b="block1",
            end_b="5prime",
            orientation="++",
        )

        assert isinstance(result, WitnessResult)
        assert result.support == 0.5  # Uninformative due to missing data

     1‚Üí"""
     2‚ÜíEvidence Aggregation Module
     3‚Üí
     4‚ÜíCombines evidence from multiple witnesses using Bayesian inference.
     5‚ÜíEach witness provides a likelihood; the aggregator computes posteriors.
     6‚Üí"""
     7‚Üí
     8‚Üífrom __future__ import annotations
     9‚Üí
    10‚Üífrom dataclasses import dataclass, field
    11‚Üífrom enum import Enum
    12‚Üífrom typing import Any, Optional
    13‚Üí
    14‚Üíimport numpy as np
    15‚Üífrom numpy.typing import NDArray
    16‚Üí
    17‚Üífrom verity.witness.base import Witness, WitnessResult
    18‚Üí
    19‚Üí
    20‚Üíclass AggregationMethod(str, Enum):
    21‚Üí    """Methods for combining evidence from multiple witnesses."""
    22‚Üí
    23‚Üí    # Multiply likelihoods (assumes independence)
    24‚Üí    PRODUCT = "product"
    25‚Üí
    26‚Üí    # Weighted average of support scores
    27‚Üí    WEIGHTED_AVERAGE = "weighted_average"
    28‚Üí
    29‚Üí    # Take minimum support (conservative)
    30‚Üí    MINIMUM = "minimum"
    31‚Üí
    32‚Üí    # Take maximum support (optimistic)
    33‚Üí    MAXIMUM = "maximum"
    34‚Üí
    35‚Üí    # Log-linear combination
    36‚Üí    LOG_LINEAR = "log_linear"
    37‚Üí
    38‚Üí
    39‚Üí@dataclass
    40‚Üíclass AggregatedEvidence:
    41‚Üí    """
    42‚Üí    Combined evidence from multiple witnesses.
    43‚Üí
    44‚Üí    Represents the posterior probability after combining all evidence.
    45‚Üí    """
    46‚Üí
    47‚Üí    # Final support score (0-1)
    48‚Üí    support: float
    49‚Üí
    50‚Üí    # Combined log-likelihood
    51‚Üí    log_likelihood: float
    52‚Üí
    53‚Üí    # Confidence in the aggregated result (0-1)
    54‚Üí    # Based on agreement between witnesses
    55‚Üí    confidence: float
    56‚Üí
    57‚Üí    # Individual witness results
    58‚Üí    witness_results: dict[str, WitnessResult] = field(default_factory=dict)
    59‚Üí
    60‚Üí    # Aggregation method used
    61‚Üí    method: AggregationMethod = AggregationMethod.PRODUCT
    62‚Üí
    63‚Üí    # Detailed metrics
    64‚Üí    metrics: dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)
    65‚Üí
    66‚Üí    def validate(self) -> list[str]:
    67‚Üí        """Validate the aggregated evidence."""
    68‚Üí        errors = []
    69‚Üí        if not 0.0 <= self.support <= 1.0:
    70‚Üí            errors.append(f"support must be in [0, 1], got {self.support}")
    71‚Üí        if not 0.0 <= self.confidence <= 1.0:
    72‚Üí            errors.append(f"confidence must be in [0, 1], got {self.confidence}")
    73‚Üí        if np.isnan(self.log_likelihood):
    74‚Üí            errors.append("log_likelihood is NaN")
    75‚Üí        return errors
    76‚Üí
    77‚Üí    @property
    78‚Üí    def is_informative(self) -> bool:
    79‚Üí        """Whether this evidence is informative (not neutral)."""
    80‚Üí        return self.confidence > 0.1 and abs(self.support - 0.5) > 0.1
    81‚Üí
    82‚Üí    @property
    83‚Üí    def verdict(self) -> str:
    84‚Üí        """Human-readable verdict based on support and confidence."""
    85‚Üí        if self.confidence < 0.3:
    86‚Üí            return "insufficient_evidence"
    87‚Üí        elif self.support > 0.8:
    88‚Üí            return "strong_support"
    89‚Üí        elif self.support > 0.6:
    90‚Üí            return "moderate_support"
    91‚Üí        elif self.support < 0.2:
    92‚Üí            return "strong_opposition"
    93‚Üí        elif self.support < 0.4:
    94‚Üí            return "moderate_opposition"
    95‚Üí        else:
    96‚Üí            return "inconclusive"
    97‚Üí
    98‚Üí
    99‚Üíclass EvidenceAggregator:
   100‚Üí    """
   101‚Üí    Aggregates evidence from multiple witnesses.
   102‚Üí
   103‚Üí    Uses Bayesian inference to combine likelihoods from different
   104‚Üí    evidence sources into posterior probabilities.
   105‚Üí    """
   106‚Üí
   107‚Üí    def __init__(
   108‚Üí        self,
   109‚Üí        witnesses: list[Witness],
   110‚Üí        weights: Optional[dict[str, float]] = None,
   111‚Üí        method: AggregationMethod = AggregationMethod.PRODUCT,
   112‚Üí        prior: float = 0.5,
   113‚Üí    ):
   114‚Üí        """
   115‚Üí        Initialize the aggregator.
   116‚Üí
   117‚Üí        Args:
   118‚Üí            witnesses: List of witnesses to aggregate
   119‚Üí            weights: Optional weights for each witness (by name)
   120‚Üí            method: Aggregation method to use
   121‚Üí            prior: Prior probability (default 0.5 = uninformative)
   122‚Üí        """
   123‚Üí        self.witnesses = {w.name: w for w in witnesses}
   124‚Üí        self.weights = weights or {w.name: 1.0 for w in witnesses}
   125‚Üí        self.method = method
   126‚Üí        self.prior = prior
   127‚Üí
   128‚Üí        # Normalize weights
   129‚Üí        total = sum(self.weights.get(name, 1.0) for name in self.witnesses)
   130‚Üí        self.weights = {
   131‚Üí            name: self.weights.get(name, 1.0) / total for name in self.witnesses
   132‚Üí        }
   133‚Üí
   134‚Üí    def aggregate_adjacency(
   135‚Üí        self,
   136‚Üí        block_a: str,
   137‚Üí        end_a: str,
   138‚Üí        block_b: str,
   139‚Üí        end_b: str,
   140‚Üí        orientation: str,
   141‚Üí    ) -> AggregatedEvidence:
   142‚Üí        """
   143‚Üí        Aggregate evidence for a proposed adjacency.
   144‚Üí
   145‚Üí        Args:
   146‚Üí            block_a: First block ID
   147‚Üí            end_a: End of first block
   148‚Üí            block_b: Second block ID
   149‚Üí            end_b: End of second block
   150‚Üí            orientation: Orientation string
   151‚Üí
   152‚Üí        Returns:
   153‚Üí            Aggregated evidence with combined support and confidence
   154‚Üí        """
   155‚Üí        # Collect evidence from each witness
   156‚Üí        results: dict[str, WitnessResult] = {}
   157‚Üí
   158‚Üí        for name, witness in self.witnesses.items():
   159‚Üí            result = witness.evaluate_adjacency(
   160‚Üí                block_a, end_a, block_b, end_b, orientation
   161‚Üí            )
   162‚Üí            results[name] = result
   163‚Üí
   164‚Üí        return self._aggregate_results(results)
   165‚Üí
   166‚Üí    def aggregate_chromosome_assignment(
   167‚Üí        self,
   168‚Üí        block_id: str,
   169‚Üí        chromosome_blocks: list[str],
   170‚Üí    ) -> AggregatedEvidence:
   171‚Üí        """
   172‚Üí        Aggregate evidence for chromosome assignment.
   173‚Üí
   174‚Üí        Args:
   175‚Üí            block_id: Block to evaluate
   176‚Üí            chromosome_blocks: Other blocks in the chromosome
   177‚Üí
   178‚Üí        Returns:
   179‚Üí            Aggregated evidence
   180‚Üí        """
   181‚Üí        results: dict[str, WitnessResult] = {}
   182‚Üí
   183‚Üí        for name, witness in self.witnesses.items():
   184‚Üí            result = witness.evaluate_chromosome_assignment(block_id, chromosome_blocks)
   185‚Üí            results[name] = result
   186‚Üí
   187‚Üí        return self._aggregate_results(results)
   188‚Üí
   189‚Üí    def _aggregate_results(
   190‚Üí        self,
   191‚Üí        results: dict[str, WitnessResult],
   192‚Üí    ) -> AggregatedEvidence:
   193‚Üí        """
   194‚Üí        Aggregate multiple witness results into combined evidence.
   195‚Üí
   196‚Üí        Args:
   197‚Üí            results: Dictionary of witness name -> result
   198‚Üí
   199‚Üí        Returns:
   200‚Üí            Aggregated evidence
   201‚Üí        """
   202‚Üí        if not results:
   203‚Üí            return AggregatedEvidence(
   204‚Üí                support=0.5,
   205‚Üí                log_likelihood=0.0,
   206‚Üí                confidence=0.0,
   207‚Üí                witness_results={},
   208‚Üí                method=self.method,
   209‚Üí            )
   210‚Üí
   211‚Üí        if self.method == AggregationMethod.PRODUCT:
   212‚Üí            return self._aggregate_product(results)
   213‚Üí        elif self.method == AggregationMethod.WEIGHTED_AVERAGE:
   214‚Üí            return self._aggregate_weighted_average(results)
   215‚Üí        elif self.method == AggregationMethod.MINIMUM:
   216‚Üí            return self._aggregate_minimum(results)
   217‚Üí        elif self.method == AggregationMethod.MAXIMUM:
   218‚Üí            return self._aggregate_maximum(results)
   219‚Üí        elif self.method == AggregationMethod.LOG_LINEAR:
   220‚Üí            return self._aggregate_log_linear(results)
   221‚Üí        else:
   222‚Üí            raise ValueError(f"Unknown aggregation method: {self.method}")
   223‚Üí
   224‚Üí    def _aggregate_product(
   225‚Üí        self,
   226‚Üí        results: dict[str, WitnessResult],
   227‚Üí    ) -> AggregatedEvidence:
   228‚Üí        """
   229‚Üí        Aggregate using product of likelihoods (Bayesian update).
   230‚Üí
   231‚Üí        P(H|E1,E2,...) ‚àù P(H) * P(E1|H) * P(E2|H) * ...
   232‚Üí        """
   233‚Üí        # Convert support scores to odds ratios
   234‚Üí        # support = P(H|E) => odds = support / (1 - support)
   235‚Üí        log_odds = np.log(self.prior / (1 - self.prior))
   236‚Üí
   237‚Üí        # Sum log-likelihoods (weighted)
   238‚Üí        total_log_likelihood = 0.0
   239‚Üí
   240‚Üí        for name, result in results.items():
   241‚Üí            weight = self.weights.get(name, 1.0 / len(results))
   242‚Üí
   243‚Üí            # Convert support to log-odds contribution
   244‚Üí            support = np.clip(result.support, 0.001, 0.999)
   245‚Üí            log_odds_contribution = np.log(support / (1 - support))
   246‚Üí
   247‚Üí            log_odds += weight * log_odds_contribution
   248‚Üí            total_log_likelihood += weight * result.log_likelihood
   249‚Üí
   250‚Üí        # Convert back to probability
   251‚Üí        support = 1.0 / (1.0 + np.exp(-log_odds))
   252‚Üí        support = float(np.clip(support, 0.0, 1.0))
   253‚Üí
   254‚Üí        # Compute confidence based on witness agreement
   255‚Üí        confidence = self._compute_confidence(results)
   256‚Üí
   257‚Üí        return AggregatedEvidence(
   258‚Üí            support=support,
   259‚Üí            log_likelihood=total_log_likelihood,
   260‚Üí            confidence=confidence,
   261‚Üí            witness_results=results,
   262‚Üí            method=AggregationMethod.PRODUCT,
   263‚Üí            metrics={
   264‚Üí                "num_witnesses": len(results),
   265‚Üí                "log_odds": log_odds,
   266‚Üí            },
   267‚Üí        )
   268‚Üí
   269‚Üí    def _aggregate_weighted_average(
   270‚Üí        self,
   271‚Üí        results: dict[str, WitnessResult],
   272‚Üí    ) -> AggregatedEvidence:
   273‚Üí        """Aggregate using weighted average of support scores."""
   274‚Üí        total_support = 0.0
   275‚Üí        total_log_likelihood = 0.0
   276‚Üí        total_weight = 0.0
   277‚Üí
   278‚Üí        for name, result in results.items():
   279‚Üí            weight = self.weights.get(name, 1.0 / len(results))
   280‚Üí            total_support += weight * result.support
   281‚Üí            total_log_likelihood += weight * result.log_likelihood
   282‚Üí            total_weight += weight
   283‚Üí
   284‚Üí        support = total_support / total_weight if total_weight > 0 else 0.5
   285‚Üí        confidence = self._compute_confidence(results)
   286‚Üí
   287‚Üí        return AggregatedEvidence(
   288‚Üí            support=float(support),
   289‚Üí            log_likelihood=total_log_likelihood,
   290‚Üí            confidence=confidence,
   291‚Üí            witness_results=results,
   292‚Üí            method=AggregationMethod.WEIGHTED_AVERAGE,
   293‚Üí        )
   294‚Üí
   295‚Üí    def _aggregate_minimum(
   296‚Üí        self,
   297‚Üí        results: dict[str, WitnessResult],
   298‚Üí    ) -> AggregatedEvidence:
   299‚Üí        """Aggregate using minimum support (conservative)."""
   300‚Üí        min_support = min(r.support for r in results.values())
   301‚Üí        total_log_likelihood = sum(r.log_likelihood for r in results.values())
   302‚Üí        confidence = self._compute_confidence(results)
   303‚Üí
   304‚Üí        return AggregatedEvidence(
   305‚Üí            support=min_support,
   306‚Üí            log_likelihood=total_log_likelihood,
   307‚Üí            confidence=confidence,
   308‚Üí            witness_results=results,
   309‚Üí            method=AggregationMethod.MINIMUM,
   310‚Üí        )
   311‚Üí
   312‚Üí    def _aggregate_maximum(
   313‚Üí        self,
   314‚Üí        results: dict[str, WitnessResult],
   315‚Üí    ) -> AggregatedEvidence:
   316‚Üí        """Aggregate using maximum support (optimistic)."""
   317‚Üí        max_support = max(r.support for r in results.values())
   318‚Üí        total_log_likelihood = sum(r.log_likelihood for r in results.values())
   319‚Üí        confidence = self._compute_confidence(results)
   320‚Üí
   321‚Üí        return AggregatedEvidence(
   322‚Üí            support=max_support,
   323‚Üí            log_likelihood=total_log_likelihood,
   324‚Üí            confidence=confidence,
   325‚Üí            witness_results=results,
   326‚Üí            method=AggregationMethod.MAXIMUM,
   327‚Üí        )
   328‚Üí
   329‚Üí    def _aggregate_log_linear(
   330‚Üí        self,
   331‚Üí        results: dict[str, WitnessResult],
   332‚Üí    ) -> AggregatedEvidence:
   333‚Üí        """
   334‚Üí        Aggregate using log-linear combination.
   335‚Üí
   336‚Üí        log P(H|E) = Œ£ w_i * log P(E_i|H) + const
   337‚Üí        """
   338‚Üí        total_log_likelihood = 0.0
   339‚Üí
   340‚Üí        for name, result in results.items():
   341‚Üí            weight = self.weights.get(name, 1.0 / len(results))
   342‚Üí            total_log_likelihood += weight * result.log_likelihood
   343‚Üí
   344‚Üí        # Convert log-likelihood to support score
   345‚Üí        # Using sigmoid transformation
   346‚Üí        support = 1.0 / (1.0 + np.exp(-total_log_likelihood / 10.0))
   347‚Üí        support = float(np.clip(support, 0.0, 1.0))
   348‚Üí
   349‚Üí        confidence = self._compute_confidence(results)
   350‚Üí
   351‚Üí        return AggregatedEvidence(
   352‚Üí            support=support,
   353‚Üí            log_likelihood=total_log_likelihood,
   354‚Üí            confidence=confidence,
   355‚Üí            witness_results=results,
   356‚Üí            method=AggregationMethod.LOG_LINEAR,
   357‚Üí        )
   358‚Üí
   359‚Üí    def _compute_confidence(
   360‚Üí        self,
   361‚Üí        results: dict[str, WitnessResult],
   362‚Üí    ) -> float:
   363‚Üí        """
   364‚Üí        Compute confidence based on witness agreement.
   365‚Üí
   366‚Üí        High confidence when witnesses agree; low when they disagree.
   367‚Üí        """
   368‚Üí        if len(results) < 2:
   369‚Üí            # Single witness - confidence based on how extreme the support is
   370‚Üí            if results:
   371‚Üí                support = list(results.values())[0].support
   372‚Üí                return float(2 * abs(support - 0.5))
   373‚Üí            return 0.0
   374‚Üí
   375‚Üí        # Multiple witnesses - use variance of support scores
   376‚Üí        supports = [r.support for r in results.values()]
   377‚Üí        mean_support = np.mean(supports)
   378‚Üí        variance = np.var(supports)
   379‚Üí
   380‚Üí        # High agreement = low variance = high confidence
   381‚Üí        # Max variance is 0.25 (when some say 0, others say 1)
   382‚Üí        agreement = 1.0 - min(1.0, variance / 0.25)
   383‚Üí
   384‚Üí        # Also consider how informative the mean is
   385‚Üí        informativeness = 2 * abs(mean_support - 0.5)
   386‚Üí
   387‚Üí        # Combine agreement and informativeness
   388‚Üí        confidence = agreement * informativeness
   389‚Üí
   390‚Üí        return float(np.clip(confidence, 0.0, 1.0))
   391‚Üí
   392‚Üí    def get_witness_weights(self) -> dict[str, float]:
   393‚Üí        """Get the current witness weights."""
   394‚Üí        return dict(self.weights)
   395‚Üí
   396‚Üí    def set_witness_weight(self, name: str, weight: float) -> None:
   397‚Üí        """Set weight for a specific witness."""
   398‚Üí        if name not in self.witnesses:
   399‚Üí            raise ValueError(f"Unknown witness: {name}")
   400‚Üí        self.weights[name] = weight
   401‚Üí
   402‚Üí        # Re-normalize
   403‚Üí        total = sum(self.weights.values())
   404‚Üí        self.weights = {k: v / total for k, v in self.weights.items()}
   405‚Üí
   406‚Üí
   407‚Üídef combine_evidence(
   408‚Üí    evidence_list: list[AggregatedEvidence],
   409‚Üí    method: AggregationMethod = AggregationMethod.PRODUCT,
   410‚Üí) -> AggregatedEvidence:
   411‚Üí    """
   412‚Üí    Combine multiple aggregated evidence objects.
   413‚Üí
   414‚Üí    Useful for meta-analysis or hierarchical inference.
   415‚Üí
   416‚Üí    Args:
   417‚Üí        evidence_list: List of aggregated evidence to combine
   418‚Üí        method: Method for combination
   419‚Üí
   420‚Üí    Returns:
   421‚Üí        Combined aggregated evidence
   422‚Üí    """
   423‚Üí    if not evidence_list:
   424‚Üí        return AggregatedEvidence(
   425‚Üí            support=0.5,
   426‚Üí            log_likelihood=0.0,
   427‚Üí            confidence=0.0,
   428‚Üí        )
   429‚Üí
   430‚Üí    if len(evidence_list) == 1:
   431‚Üí        return evidence_list[0]
   432‚Üí
   433‚Üí    supports = [e.support for e in evidence_list]
   434‚Üí    log_likelihoods = [e.log_likelihood for e in evidence_list]
   435‚Üí    confidences = [e.confidence for e in evidence_list]
   436‚Üí
   437‚Üí    if method == AggregationMethod.PRODUCT:
   438‚Üí        # Bayesian combination
   439‚Üí        log_odds = sum(
   440‚Üí            np.log(np.clip(s, 0.001, 0.999) / (1 - np.clip(s, 0.001, 0.999)))
   441‚Üí            for s in supports
   442‚Üí        )
   443‚Üí        support = 1.0 / (1.0 + np.exp(-log_odds))
   444‚Üí    elif method == AggregationMethod.WEIGHTED_AVERAGE:
   445‚Üí        # Weight by confidence
   446‚Üí        total_weight = sum(confidences) or 1.0
   447‚Üí        support = sum(s * c for s, c in zip(supports, confidences)) / total_weight
   448‚Üí    elif method == AggregationMethod.MINIMUM:
   449‚Üí        support = min(supports)
   450‚Üí    elif method == AggregationMethod.MAXIMUM:
   451‚Üí        support = max(supports)
   452‚Üí    else:
   453‚Üí        support = np.mean(supports)
   454‚Üí
   455‚Üí    # Combine log-likelihoods
   456‚Üí    total_ll = sum(log_likelihoods)
   457‚Üí
   458‚Üí    # Confidence is based on agreement
   459‚Üí    variance = np.var(supports)
   460‚Üí    confidence = 1.0 - min(1.0, variance / 0.25)
   461‚Üí    confidence *= np.mean(confidences)  # Also consider input confidences
   462‚Üí
   463‚Üí    # Merge all witness results
   464‚Üí    all_results = {}
   465‚Üí    for i, e in enumerate(evidence_list):
   466‚Üí        for name, result in e.witness_results.items():
   467‚Üí            key = f"{name}_{i}" if name in all_results else name
   468‚Üí            all_results[key] = result
   469‚Üí
   470‚Üí    return AggregatedEvidence(
   471‚Üí        support=float(np.clip(support, 0.0, 1.0)),
   472‚Üí        log_likelihood=total_ll,
   473‚Üí        confidence=float(np.clip(confidence, 0.0, 1.0)),
   474‚Üí        witness_results=all_results,
   475‚Üí        method=method,
   476‚Üí        metrics={"num_combined": len(evidence_list)},
   477‚Üí    )
   478‚Üí

"""Integration tests for multi-witness evidence aggregation.

Tests combining Hi-C and Telomere witnesses for genome assembly validation.
"""

import numpy as np
import pytest

from verity.witness.base import Witness, WitnessResult
from verity.witness.hic import HiCWitness, BlockPosition as HiCBlockPosition, DecayParameters
from verity.witness.telomere import TelomereWitness, BlockPosition as TelomereBlockPosition
from verity.infer.aggregator import EvidenceAggregator, AggregationMethod


class TestMultiWitnessAggregation:
    """Tests for combining multiple witness types."""

    @pytest.fixture
    def hic_witness(self):
        """Create a simple Hi-C witness for testing."""
        # Create a 10x10 contact matrix with realistic decay
        size = 10
        resolution = 10000
        matrix = np.zeros((size, size))

        # Add contacts with distance decay
        alpha = 1.0
        for i in range(size):
            for j in range(size):
                if i != j:
                    distance = abs(i - j) * resolution
                    matrix[i, j] = 1000 / (distance / 10000) ** alpha
                else:
                    matrix[i, j] = 100  # Diagonal

        # Block positions
        block_positions = {
            "block_A": HiCBlockPosition(
                start_bin=0, end_bin=5, contig="chr1",
                start_bp=0, end_bp=50000
            ),
            "block_B": HiCBlockPosition(
                start_bin=5, end_bin=10, contig="chr1",
                start_bp=50000, end_bp=100000
            ),
        }

        return HiCWitness(
            contact_matrix=matrix,
            resolution=resolution,
            block_positions=block_positions,
            parameters=DecayParameters(alpha=1.0, beta=1.0, gamma=1e-6),
        )

    @pytest.fixture
    def telomere_witness_clean(self):
        """Create a telomere witness with no telomeres at junction."""
        # Sequence with telomeres only at true ends
        telomere = "TTAGGG" * 10
        middle = "ATCG" * 24970  # ~100kb middle
        sequences = {
            "chr1": telomere + middle + "CCCTAA" * 10,
        }
        block_positions = {
            "block_A": TelomereBlockPosition(contig="chr1", start=60, end=50000),
            "block_B": TelomereBlockPosition(contig="chr1", start=50000, end=99940),
        }

        return TelomereWitness(
            sequences=sequences,
            block_positions=block_positions,
            search_window=10000,
        )

    @pytest.fixture
    def telomere_witness_misjoin(self):
        """Create a telomere witness with telomere at junction (misjoin)."""
        # Telomere in the middle - indicates misjoin
        part1 = "ATCG" * 12500  # 50kb
        telomere = "TTAGGG" * 10
        part2 = "ATCG" * 12485  # ~50kb
        sequences = {
            "chr1": part1 + telomere + part2,
        }
        block_positions = {
            "block_A": TelomereBlockPosition(contig="chr1", start=0, end=50000),
            "block_B": TelomereBlockPosition(contig="chr1", start=50000, end=100000),
        }

        return TelomereWitness(
            sequences=sequences,
            block_positions=block_positions,
            search_window=10000,
        )

    def test_two_witnesses_agreeing(self, hic_witness, telomere_witness_clean):
        """Test aggregation when both witnesses agree (good adjacency)."""
        aggregator = EvidenceAggregator(
            witnesses=[hic_witness, telomere_witness_clean],
            method=AggregationMethod.PRODUCT,
        )

        # Evaluate adjacency that both witnesses support
        result = aggregator.aggregate_adjacency(
            block_a="block_A",
            end_a="3prime",
            block_b="block_B",
            end_b="5prime",
            orientation="++",
        )

        assert result.support >= 0.5  # Should be supported
        assert len(result.witness_results) == 2
        assert "hic" in result.witness_results
        assert "telomere" in result.witness_results

    def test_two_witnesses_disagreeing(self, hic_witness, telomere_witness_misjoin):
        """Test aggregation when witnesses disagree (telomere indicates misjoin)."""
        aggregator = EvidenceAggregator(
            witnesses=[hic_witness, telomere_witness_misjoin],
            method=AggregationMethod.PRODUCT,
        )

        # Evaluate adjacency - Hi-C may support but telomere opposes
        result = aggregator.aggregate_adjacency(
            block_a="block_A",
            end_a="3prime",
            block_b="block_B",
            end_b="5prime",
            orientation="++",
        )

        # Telomere at junction should lower support
        telomere_result = result.witness_results["telomere"]
        assert telomere_result.support < 0.5  # Telomere opposes

        # With product aggregation, strong opposition dominates
        # Support should be reduced from Hi-C alone

    def test_weighted_aggregation(self, hic_witness, telomere_witness_misjoin):
        """Test weighted aggregation giving more weight to telomere."""
        # Give telomere witness 3x weight (telomeres are strong evidence)
        aggregator = EvidenceAggregator(
            witnesses=[hic_witness, telomere_witness_misjoin],
            weights={"hic": 1.0, "telomere": 3.0},
            method=AggregationMethod.WEIGHTED_AVERAGE,
        )

        result = aggregator.aggregate_adjacency(
            block_a="block_A",
            end_a="3prime",
            block_b="block_B",
            end_b="5prime",
            orientation="++",
        )

        # With higher telomere weight, support should be lower
        telomere_support = result.witness_results["telomere"].support
        assert telomere_support < 0.5  # Telomere opposes

    def test_minimum_aggregation_conservative(self, hic_witness, telomere_witness_misjoin):
        """Test minimum aggregation (conservative - takes worst case)."""
        aggregator = EvidenceAggregator(
            witnesses=[hic_witness, telomere_witness_misjoin],
            method=AggregationMethod.MINIMUM,
        )

        result = aggregator.aggregate_adjacency(
            block_a="block_A",
            end_a="3prime",
            block_b="block_B",
            end_b="5prime",
            orientation="++",
        )

        # Minimum should take the telomere's low support
        telomere_support = result.witness_results["telomere"].support
        assert result.support == telomere_support

    def test_aggregation_provides_confidence(self, hic_witness, telomere_witness_clean):
        """Test that aggregation computes confidence metric."""
        aggregator = EvidenceAggregator(
            witnesses=[hic_witness, telomere_witness_clean],
            method=AggregationMethod.PRODUCT,
        )

        result = aggregator.aggregate_adjacency(
            block_a="block_A",
            end_a="3prime",
            block_b="block_B",
            end_b="5prime",
            orientation="++",
        )

        # Confidence should be computed
        assert 0.0 <= result.confidence <= 1.0

    def test_single_witness_works(self, hic_witness):
        """Test aggregation with single witness."""
        aggregator = EvidenceAggregator(
            witnesses=[hic_witness],
            method=AggregationMethod.PRODUCT,
        )

        result = aggregator.aggregate_adjacency(
            block_a="block_A",
            end_a="3prime",
            block_b="block_B",
            end_b="5prime",
            orientation="++",
        )

        assert len(result.witness_results) == 1
        assert "hic" in result.witness_results

    def test_empty_witnesses_handled(self):
        """Test aggregation with no witnesses."""
        aggregator = EvidenceAggregator(
            witnesses=[],
            method=AggregationMethod.PRODUCT,
        )

        result = aggregator.aggregate_adjacency(
            block_a="block_A",
            end_a="3prime",
            block_b="block_B",
            end_b="5prime",
            orientation="++",
        )

        assert result.support == 0.5  # Uninformative
        assert result.confidence == 0.0


class TestWitnessInterfaceCompliance:
    """Test that all witness types comply with the interface."""

    def test_telomere_witness_interface(self):
        """Test TelomereWitness implements Witness interface."""
        sequences = {"test": "TTAGGG" * 10 + "N" * 1000}
        blocks = {"block1": TelomereBlockPosition("test", 0, 1060)}

        witness = TelomereWitness(sequences=sequences, block_positions=blocks)

        # Check interface methods exist
        assert hasattr(witness, "name")
        assert hasattr(witness, "evaluate_adjacency")
        assert hasattr(witness, "evaluate_chromosome_assignment")
        assert hasattr(witness, "get_parameters")

        # Check they work
        assert witness.name == "telomere"

        result = witness.evaluate_adjacency(
            "block1", "3prime", "block1", "5prime", "++"
        )
        assert isinstance(result, WitnessResult)

        result = witness.evaluate_chromosome_assignment("block1", [])
        assert isinstance(result, WitnessResult)

        params = witness.get_parameters()
        assert isinstance(params, dict)

    def test_hic_witness_interface(self):
        """Test HiCWitness implements Witness interface."""
        matrix = np.eye(5) * 100
        blocks = {
            "block1": HiCBlockPosition(
                start_bin=0, end_bin=2, contig="chr1",
                start_bp=0, end_bp=20000
            ),
            "block2": HiCBlockPosition(
                start_bin=2, end_bin=5, contig="chr1",
                start_bp=20000, end_bp=50000
            ),
        }

        witness = HiCWitness(
            contact_matrix=matrix,
            resolution=10000,
            block_positions=blocks,
        )

        # Check interface methods
        assert hasattr(witness, "name")
        assert witness.name == "hic"

        result = witness.evaluate_adjacency(
            "block1", "3prime", "block2", "5prime", "++"
        )
        assert isinstance(result, WitnessResult)

        params = witness.get_parameters()
        assert isinstance(params, dict)


class TestChromosomeAssignmentMultiWitness:
    """Test chromosome assignment with multiple witnesses."""

    def test_complete_chromosome_both_witnesses(self):
        """Test complete chromosome evaluation with both witnesses."""
        # Hi-C with two blocks showing chromosome structure
        matrix = np.array([
            [100, 50, 40, 10, 5],
            [50, 100, 60, 8, 4],
            [40, 60, 100, 6, 3],
            [10, 8, 6, 100, 50],
            [5, 4, 3, 50, 100],
        ], dtype=float)

        hic_blocks = {
            "block_A": HiCBlockPosition(0, 3, "chr1", 0, 30000),
            "block_B": HiCBlockPosition(3, 5, "chr1", 30000, 50000),
        }

        hic_witness = HiCWitness(
            contact_matrix=matrix,
            resolution=10000,
            block_positions=hic_blocks,
        )

        # Telomere witness - complete chromosome
        sequences = {
            "chr1": "TTAGGG" * 10 + "N" * 49820 + "CCCTAA" * 10,
        }
        telomere_blocks = {
            "block_A": TelomereBlockPosition("chr1", 0, 30000),
            "block_B": TelomereBlockPosition("chr1", 30000, 50000),

            sequences=sequences,
            block_positions=telomere_blocks,
            search_window=10000,
        )

        aggregator = EvidenceAggregator(
            witnesses=[hic_witness, telomere_witness],
            method=AggregationMethod.PRODUCT,
        )

        result = aggregator.aggregate_chromosome_assignment(
            block_id="block_A",
            chromosome_blocks=["block_B"],
        )

        # Both should support this being a valid chromosome
        assert result.support > 0.5
        assert len(result.witness_results) == 2

"""Integration tests for multi-witness evidence aggregation.

Tests combining Hi-C and Telomere witnesses for genome assembly validation.
"""

import numpy as np
import pytest

from verity.witness.base import Witness, WitnessResult
from verity.witness.hic import HiCWitness, BlockPosition as HiCBlockPosition, DecayParameters
from verity.witness.telomere import TelomereWitness, BlockPosition as TelomereBlockPosition
from verity.infer.aggregator import EvidenceAggregator, AggregationMethod


class TestMultiWitnessAggregation:
    """Tests for combining multiple witness types."""

    @pytest.fixture
    def hic_witness(self):
        """Create a simple Hi-C witness for testing."""
        # Create a 10x10 contact matrix with realistic decay
        size = 10
        resolution = 10000
        matrix = np.zeros((size, size))

        # Add contacts with distance decay
        alpha = 1.0
        for i in range(size):
            for j in range(size):
                if i != j:
                    distance = abs(i - j) * resolution
                    matrix[i, j] = 1000 / (distance / 10000) ** alpha
                else:
                    matrix[i, j] = 100  # Diagonal

        # Block positions
        block_positions = {
            "block_A": HiCBlockPosition(
                start_bin=0, end_bin=5, contig="chr1",
                start_bp=0, end_bp=50000
            ),
            "block_B": HiCBlockPosition(
                start_bin=5, end_bin=10, contig="chr1",
                start_bp=50000, end_bp=100000
            ),
        }

        return HiCWitness(

"""Integration tests for multi-witness evidence aggregation.

Tests combining Hi-C and Telomere witnesses for genome assembly validation.
"""

import numpy as np
import pytest

from verity.witness.base import Witness, WitnessResult
from verity.witness.hic import HiCWitness, BlockPosition as HiCBlockPosition, DecayParameters
from verity.witness.telomere import TelomereWitness, BlockPosition as TelomereBlockPosition
from verity.infer.aggregator import EvidenceAggregator, AggregationMethod


class TestMultiWitnessAggregation:
    """Tests for combining multiple witness types."""

    @pytest.fixture
    def hic_witness(self):
        """Create a simple Hi-C witness for testing."""
        # Create a 10x10 contact matrix with realistic decay
        size = 10
        resolution = 10000
        matrix = np.zeros((size, size))

        # Add contacts with distance decay
        alpha = 1.0
        for i in range(size):
            for j in range(size):
                if i != j:
                    distance = abs(i - j) * resolution
                    matrix[i, j] = 1000 / (distance / 10000) ** alpha
                else:
                    matrix[i, j] = 100  # Diagonal

        # Block positions - Hi-C uses block_id, start_bin, end_bin, length
        block_positions = {
            "block_A": HiCBlockPosition(
                block_id="block_A",
                start_bin=0,
                end_bin=5,
                length=50000,
            ),
            "block_B": HiCBlockPosition(
                block_id="block_B",
                start_bin=5,
                end_bin=10,
                length=50000,
            ),
        }

        return HiCWitness(
            contact_matrix=matrix,
            resolution=resolution,
            block_positions=block_positions,
            parameters=DecayParameters(alpha=1.0, beta=1.0, gamma=1e-6),
        )

    def test_minimum_aggregation_conservative(self, hic_witness, telomere_witness_misjoin):
        """Test minimum aggregation (conservative - takes worst case)."""

    def test_minimum_aggregation_conservative(self, hic_witness, telomere_witness_misjoin):
        """Test minimum aggregation (conservative - takes worst case)."""
        aggregator = EvidenceAggregator(
            witnesses=[hic_witness, telomere_witness_misjoin],
            method=AggregationMethod.MINIMUM,
        )

        result = aggregator.aggregate_adjacency(
            block_a="block_A",
            end_a="3prime",
            block_b="block_B",
            end_b="5prime",
            orientation="++",
        )

        # Minimum should take the lowest support between witnesses
        hic_support = result.witness_results["hic"].support
        telomere_support = result.witness_results["telomere"].support
        assert result.support == min(hic_support, telomere_support)
